Provide a short reasoning before deciding.

[planner_qa_rationale_imaginator] **Reasoning**  
The goal is to have *all* peppers on the table.  
- **pepper_4** is already on the table.  
- **pepper_3** is in the inventory and can be dropped on the table with one simple “drop” action.  
- **pepper_5** remains on the floor; it can be picked up and then dropped on the table with two more actions (move → take → move → drop).  

All required actions are straightforward, no obstacles or constraints have appeared, and the remaining steps are minimal. Therefore the plan is still on track and can be completed.

**Answer:** Yes, the plan still looks promising.

To satisfy the goal you need to place both remaining peppers on the table. The shortest sequence is to drop the pepper you are already holding, then retrieve the last pepper and put it on the table.
